                                 WHERE(Document Type=CONST(Return Order));
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lFormatAddress@1000000002 : Codeunit 365;
                                BEGIN
                                  mSalesPrintoutToolkit.SetSalesHeader(dSalesHeader);

                                  mTitle := STRSUBSTNO(tTitle, dSalesHeader."No.");

                                  lFormatAddress.Company(mCompanyAddress, mCompanyInformation);
                                  lFormatAddress.SalesHeaderSellTo(mSellToAddress, dSalesHeader);
                                  lFormatAddress.SalesHeaderBillTo(mBillToAddress, dSalesHeader);
                                  lFormatAddress.SalesHeaderShipTo(mShipToAddress, dSalesHeader);

                                  mSalesPrintoutToolkit.ContactInformation(mSellToContact);
                                  mSalesPrintoutToolkit.CurrencyInformation(mCurrencyText, mCurrencyFactorText, mAmountText, mAmountInclVatText);
                                  mSalesPrintoutToolkit.Summary(mAmount, mAmountInclVat, mAmountInWordsText);

                                  mSalespersonText := mSalesPrintoutToolkit.SalespersonPurchaserText();
                                  mPaymentTermsText := mSalesPrintoutToolkit.PaymentTermsText();
                                  mPaymentMethodText := mSalesPrintoutToolkit.PaymentMethodText();
                                  mShipmentMethodText := mSalesPrintoutToolkit.ShipmentMethodText();
                                  mShippingAgentText := mSalesPrintoutToolkit.ShippingAgentText();
                                  mShippingAgentServiceText := mSalesPrintoutToolkit.ShippingAgentServiceText();
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Document Type,No.,Sell-to Customer No.,Document Date,Posting Date }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
</Code>
